	  var c = ca[i];

    <div class="design-system ds-container copy-block-module">
        <div class="ds-text">
            
            
                <div class="ds-text-paragraph">
                    <p>Bath and Body Works is your go-to place for self-care <a href="/c/gifts/gift-sets">gifts</a> that surprise and delight. From iconic home fragrances found in Bath and Body Works <a href="/g/all-candles">candles</a> to the moisturizing skin care of Bath and Body Works <a href="/c/body-care/body-lotion">lotion</a>, we make picking out your perfect something special a sensational experience. Try a gourmand for something oh so sweet, a floral for something classically romantic, or check out <a href="/g/mens-shop">The Men&rsquo;s Shop</a> for something more earthy. Once you find your signature scent, grab a Bath and Body Works perfume, lather it up with Bath and Body Works <a href="/c/hand-soaps-sanitizers/all-hand-soaps">hand soap</a> or plug it in so it&rsquo;s always on with Bath and Body Works <a href="/c/home-fragrance/all-wallflowers">Wallflowers&reg;</a>.</p>

<p>&nbsp;</p>

<p>What&rsquo;s a store full of self-care gifts without a spa-worthy collection? Whether you&rsquo;re looking for fragrances to get the vibe right or body care items to get your skin right, our <a href="/t/wellness">wellness</a> selection has what you want. Don&rsquo;t worry if your at-home spa day suddenly becomes an at-home work day. Check out our <a href="/c/laundry-care/all-laundry">laundry</a> products that turn your chore into a load of self-care. And for those moments when you have to leave home, don&rsquo;t forget to grab a <a href="/c/hand-soaps-sanitizers/pocketbac-hand-sanitizers">PocketBac</a> for some easy, clean fragrance fun on the go. They&rsquo;re the most popular Bath and Body Works <a href="/c/hand-soaps-sanitizers/all-hand-sanitizers">hand sanitizer</a> for a reason.</p>
                </div>
